   <script>
    try {
        if (!window.localStorage || !window.sessionStorage) {
            throw new Error();
        }

        localStorage.setItem('storage_test', 1);
        localStorage.removeItem('storage_test');
    } catch(e) {
        (function () {
            var Storage = function (type) {
                var data;

                function createCookie(name, value, days) {
                    var date, expires;

                    if (days) {
                        date = new Date();
                        date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                        expires = '; expires=' + date.toGMTString();
                    } else {
                        expires = '';
                    }
                    document.cookie = name + '=' + value+expires+'; path=/';
                }

                function readCookie(name) {
                    var nameEQ = name + '=',
                        ca = document.cookie.split(';'),
                        i = 0,
                        c;

                    for (i=0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                        c = ca[i];

                        while (c.charAt(0) === ' ') {
                            c = c.substring(1,c.length);
                        }

                        if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) === 0) {
                            return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
                        }
                    }

                    return null;
                }

                function setData(data) {
                    data = encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(data));
                    createCookie(type === 'session' ? getSessionName() : 'localStorage', data, 365);
                }

                function clearData() {
                    createCookie(type === 'session' ? getSessionName() : 'localStorage', '', 365);
                }

                function getData() {
                    var data = type === 'session' ? readCookie(getSessionName()) : readCookie('localStorage');

                    return data ? JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(data)) : {};
                }

                function getSessionName() {
                    if (!window.name) {
                        window.name = new Date().getTime();
                    }

                    return 'sessionStorage' + window.name;
                }

                data = getData();

                return {
                    length: 0,
                    clear: function () {
                        data = {};
                        this.length = 0;
                        clearData();
                    },

                    getItem: function (key) {
                        return data[key] === undefined ? null : data[key];
                    },

                    key: function (i) {
                        var ctr = 0,
                            k;

                        for (k in data) {
                            if (ctr.toString() === i.toString()) {
                                return k;
                            } else {
                                ctr++
                            }
                        }

                        return null;
                    },

                    removeItem: function (key) {
                        delete data[key];
                        this.length--;
                        setData(data);
                    },

                    setItem: function (key, value) {
                        data[key] = value.toString();
                        this.length++;
                        setData(data);
                    }
                };
            };

            window.localStorage.__proto__ = window.localStorage = new Storage('local');
            window.sessionStorage.__proto__ = window.sessionStorage = new Storage('session');
        })();
    }
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    require(['jquery','underscore'],function($,_){

	// å¯¼èˆªæ æ»šåŠ¨æ‚¬æµ®

	function initScrollSticky(){
		var num = $('.header-container .header-content').outerHeight();
			if ($(this).scrollTop() > num){
				$(".header-container").addClass("sticky-top");
				$("#page-back-top").removeClass('hide');
			}else{
				$(".header-container").removeClass("sticky-top");
				$("#page-back-top").addClass('hide');
			}
	}



	// åˆå§‹åŒ–èœå•æ 
	function initSlidemenu (){
		// ç§»åŠ¨è®¾å¤‡äº‹ä»¶èœå•æ å±•å¼€äº‹ä»¶ç»‘å®š
			if($(window).width() <= 768){
				$(".header-container").removeClass("sticky-top");
				$(document).off("click",".menu-item-title .fa").on("click",".menu-item-title .fa",function(){
					var $submenuItem = 	$(this).parents(".menu-item");
					var $submenu1 =  		$submenuItem.find(".submenu-container[data-level='1']");
					if(!$submenu1.length) return ;
					var isOpen = $submenu1.attr('collapse') == 'open';
					if(isOpen){
						$submenuItem.removeClass('active') ;
						$(this).removeClass('active');
						$submenu1.attr('collapse','closed');
					} else{
						$submenuItem.addClass('active');
						$(this).addClass('active');
						$submenu1.attr('collapse','open');
					} 
				})

				$(document).off("click",".submenu-item .submenu-item-title .fa").on("click",".submenu-item .submenu-item-title .fa",function(){
					var $submenuItem = $(this).parents(".submenu-item");
					var $submenu1 = $submenuItem.find(".submenu-container").length ? $submenuItem.find(".submenu-container").eq(0) : false;
					if(!$submenu1) return ;
					var level = $submenu1.attr('data-level');
					if($submenuItem.hasClass('active')){
						$submenuItem.removeClass('active') ;
						$(this).removeClass('active');
						$submenu1.attr('collapse','closed');
					} else{
						$submenuItem.addClass('active');
						$(this).addClass('active');
						$submenu1.attr('collapse','open');
					} 
					
				})
			
			
			}else{
				// pcç«¯è®¾å¤‡äº‹ä»¶ç»‘å®š
				// ä¸€çº§èœå•å±•å¼€äº‹ä»¶ç»‘å®š
				$(document).off("mouseenter",".menu-item").on("mouseenter",".menu-item",function(){	
					var $submenu1 = $(this).find(".submenu-container[data-level='1']");
					if(!$submenu1.length) return ;
						if($submenu1.hasClass('horizon')){
							var $targetDom = $(".header-container-wrapper")	
							var offset = $targetDom.length ? $targetDom.offset() : 0;
							$submenu1.offset({
								left : $targetDom.find('.header-content').offset().left ,
								// top  : "100%"
							}).attr('set-position',true);
						}
					
					$('.submenu-container[data-level="1"]').attr('collapse','closed');
					$submenu1.attr('collapse','open');
				})
				
				// äºŒçº§èœå•å±•å¼€äº‹ä»¶ç»‘å®š
				$(document).off('mouseenter',".submenu-item").on("mouseenter",".submenu-item",function(){
					var $submenu1 = $(this).find(".submenu-container").length ? $(this).find(".submenu-container").eq(0) : false;
					if(!$submenu1) return ;
					var level = $submenu1.attr('data-level');
					
					// æ°´å¹³äºŒçº§èœå•å®šä½left
					if($submenu1.hasClass('horizon')){
						var $targetDom = $(this).parents('.submenu-container').length ? $(this).parents('.submenu-container').eq(0) : null;
						var offset = $targetDom ? $targetDom.offset() : 0;
						$submenu1.offset({
							left : offset.left	
						}).attr('set-position',true);
					}
					
					$('.submenu-container[data-level="'+level+'"]').attr('collapse','closed');
					$submenu1.attr('collapse','open');


					// åž‚ç›´äºŒçº§èœå• è®¡ç®—æ˜¯å¦è§¦åº•
					if($submenu1.hasClass('calculate-postion') && !$submenu1.attr('set-position')){
						var locationSubmenuTT = setTimeout(function(){
							try{
								var h = $submenu1.height();
								var headerH = $(".header-container-wrapper").height();
								var offseTop = $submenu1.offset().top;
								var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();
								var topDistance = offseTop - scrollTop;		// é¡¶éƒ¨è·ç¦»
								var bottomDistance = $(window).height() - (topDistance + h); // åº•éƒ¨è·ç¦»
																						
								if(topDistance < headerH && topDistance > 0 ){
									$submenu1.css('transform','translateY('+(  headerH - topDistance  - h/2)+'px)');
								}else if(topDistance <= 0){
									$submenu1.css('transform','translateY('+( Math.abs(topDistance)  + headerH   - h/2)+'px)');
								}else if(bottomDistance < 0 ){
									$submenu1.css({
										'transform' : 'translateY('+ (bottomDistance - 1 - h/2) +'px)',
									});
								}
								$submenu1.attr('set-position',true);
								clearTimeout(locationSubmenuTT);
							}catch(positionErr){
								console.log('submenu2 location error :'+positionErr);
								clearTimeout(locationSubmenuTT);
							}
						},150)
					}		
					
				})

				// ä¸€çº§èœå•å…³é—­
				$(document).on("mouseleave",".menu-item",function(){
					var $submenu1 = $(this).find(".submenu-container");
					$submenu1.attr('collapse','closed');
				})


				// äºŒçº§èœå•å…³é—­
				$(document).on("mouseleave",".submenu-item",function(){
					var $submenu1 = $(this).children(".submenu-container").length ? $(this).children(".submenu-container").eq(0) : false;
					if(!$submenu1) return ;
					var level = $submenu1.attr('data-level');
					$('.submenu-container[data-level="'+level+'"]').removeAttr('is-prev');
					$submenu1.attr('collapse','closed');

				})
			}
	}



	//åˆå§‹åŒ–èœå•æ 
	initSlidemenu();
	
	// è¿”å›žé¡¶éƒ¨æŒ‰é’®äº‹ä»¶ç»‘å®š
	$(document).on('click',"#page-back-top",function(){
		$('body,html').animate({'scrollTop':0})
	})

	// æ»šåŠ¨ç›‘å¬

	$(window).on('scroll',function() {
			initScrollSticky();
	});

	// å°ºå¯¸å˜åŒ–ç›‘å¬
	$(window).on('resize',_.throttle(function(){
		$(".submenu-container").removeAttr('set-position');
		$(".submenu-container").removeAttr('style');
		initSlidemenu();
	},1000))

});



/*  modify by huchuanwei */

var visitedPages = parseInt(localStorage.getItem("visitedPages"));
 if(isNaN(visitedPages)){
	 localStorage.setItem("visitedPages",0)
}

function findError(){
	var timer = setInterval(function(){
		var ele = document.querySelector("div[data-ui-id=checkout-cart-validationmessages-message-error]");
		if(ele){
			var errMsg = ele.innerHTML.length?ele.innerHTML:"Invalid login or password!";
			if (window.dataLayer) {
				dataLayer.push({
					signInType: 'Email',
					signInFailed:errMsg,
					event: 'SignInFailed'
				});
			}
			clearInterval(timer)
		}
	},500)
}

// if is logined 

	localStorage.setItem("visitedPages",0)
	findError();

    require([
			'jquery',

                if($(".slider_homepage4slider").parents(".nav-banner").length){
                    $(window).on("load",function(){
                        var navBannerOwlConfig = 
                                {autoPlay:true,navigation:true,stopOnHover:true,pagination:true,scrollPerPage:true,items:1,rewindSpeed:500,paginationSpeed:500,slideSpeed:500,itemsDesktop:[1199,1],itemsDesktopSmall:[980,1],itemsTablet:[768,1],                                     afterInit: lazyLoadImages,
                                    afterAction: lazyLoadImages	,
                                    afterMove :  lazyLoadImages
                                }
                            navBannerOwlConfig["autoPlay"] = true; 
                        $(".slider_homepage4slider .owl").owlCarousel(navBannerOwlConfig);
                        $(".slider_homepage4slider .owl .owl-item .banner_item").show();
					})
                }else{
                    $(".slider_homepage4slider .owl").owlCarousel(
                        {autoPlay:true,navigation:true,stopOnHover:true,pagination:true,scrollPerPage:true,items:1,rewindSpeed:500,paginationSpeed:500,slideSpeed:500,itemsDesktop:[1199,1],itemsDesktopSmall:[980,1],itemsTablet:[768,1],                            afterInit: lazyLoadImages,
                            afterAction: lazyLoadImages,
                        }
                    );
                }
                
                function lazyLoadImages(ele) {
                    $('body').find('picture.lazy').lazy({
                        attribute: 'data-original',
                        visibleOnly: true,
                    });

                    /* modify by chuanwei */
                    var activeIndex = $(ele).find(".owl-pagination .owl-page.active").index();
                    if(activeIndex >= 0){
                        var activeItem = $(ele).find(".owl-wrapper .owl-item").get(activeIndex);
                        if($(activeItem).length){
                            var currentImg =  $(activeItem).find("img");
                            if($(currentImg).length && $(currentImg).attr("data-src")){
                                $(currentImg).attr("src", $(currentImg).attr("data-src"))
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            
                
                $(".slider_homepage4slider .owl .owl-item .banner_item").show();
			});

                var cols = $(_this).parents(".owl-wrapper").find(".owl-item") ? $(_this).parents(".owl-wrapper").find(".owl-item").length : 0;  // total cols count
                var rowIndex = $(_this).parents(".product_row").index(); // row locate
                var colIndex = $(_this).parents(".owl-item").index();  // col locate
                var position;
                if (cols && colIndex >= 0 && rowIndex >= 0) {
                    position = rowIndex * cols + colIndex + 1;
                }
                /*modify by huchuanwei in 2019/07/22 END*/
                dataLayer.push({
                    'event': 'ProductClick-Home',
                    'ecommerce': {
                        'click': {
                            'actionField': {'list': cateTitle},
                            'products': [{
                                'id': $(_this).attr('data-id'),
                                'name': $(_this).attr('data-name'),
                                'price': $(_this).attr('data-price'),
                                // 'position': $(_this).attr('data-position'),
                                'position': position >= 0 ? position : $(_this).attr('data-position'),
                                'category': $(_this).attr('data-category').replace(/((\n+)|(\t+)|(\/+$)|(^\s+)|(\s+$))/g, ""),
                                'variant': $(_this).attr('data-sku')
                            }]
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        });

                    'quickViewProduct': $(this).attr('data-name') + ' - ' + $(this).attr('data-id'),
                    'event': 'quickView'

            }
        })

    });

   <script>
    var checkPrint = function() {
	if(document.getElementById("pagePrint")){return}
		var link = document.createElement("link");
		if(/mg1\.seeed\.cc/.test(location.hostname)){
			link.setAttribute("href","/static/frontend/bs_complex/bs_complex5/en_US/css/print.css");
		}else if(/seeedstudio\.vip/.test(location.hostname) || /seeedstudio\.com/.test(location.hostname)){
			link.setAttribute("href","/static/frontend/bs_complex/bs_complex5/en_US/css/print.min.css");
		}
		
		link.setAttribute("media","print");
		link.setAttribute("rel","stylesheet");
		link.setAttribute("type","text/css");
		link.id = "pagePrint";
		document.head.appendChild(link);	
};

if (window.matchMedia) {
	var mediaQueryList = window.matchMedia('print');
    mediaQueryList.addListener(function(mql) {
        if (mql.matches) {
            checkPrint();
        }
    });
}

if(window.addEventListener){
	window.addEventListener("beforeprint",checkPrint)
}else if(window.attachEvent){
	window.attachEvent("beforeprint",beforePrint)
}

	function setChekoutFooter(){
		var footer = $(".footer-container");
		/* if(footer.length){
			footer.addClass("checkout-footer-container");
		}; */
		var footerList = $(".footer-bottom .bottom-info .policy .footer-list");
		if(footerList.length){
			$(".footer-bottom").addClass("checkout-footer-bottom");
			footerList.append("<li class='fl shipping'> <a href='https://www.seeedstudio.com/get_help/ShippingOrder' target='_blank'>Shipping & Order</a></li><li class='fl warranty'> <a href='https://www.seeedstudio.com/get_help/ReturnsRefund' target='_blank'>Warranty & Returns</a></li>")
		}
	}
	if(/checkout/.test(location.pathname)){
		setChekoutFooter();
	}
})

                            "appendTo": "",

                    }
                }
            }
        }
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    require(['jquery'], function ($) {
            var recaptcha = [],
                formsToProtect = 'form[action*="customer/account/createpost"],form[action*="newsletter/subscriber/new"],form[action*="review/product/post"],form[action*="contact/index/post"],form[action*="recatpcha/index/check"]';

            window.formToProtectOnPage = [];
            $.each($(formsToProtect), function (index, formToProtect) {
                window.formToProtectOnPage.push(formToProtect);
            });

            if (window.formToProtectOnPage.length) {
                var recaptchaScript = document.createElement('script');
                recaptchaScript.src = 'https://www.recaptcha.net/recaptcha/api.js?onload=amInvisibleCaptchaOnloadCallback&render=explicit';
                recaptchaScript.attributes = 'async defer';
                document.body.appendChild(recaptchaScript);
            }

            window.amInvisibleCaptchaOnloadCallback = function () {
                for (var i = 0; i < window.formToProtectOnPage.length; i++) {
                    var tokenInput = document.createElement('input');
                    tokenInput.type = 'hidden';
                    tokenInput.name = 'amasty_invisible_token';
                    window.formToProtectOnPage[i].appendChild(tokenInput);
                }

                var id = "";
                if (id) {
                    var additionalForm = document.getElementById(id).form;
                    if (additionalForm) {
                        window.formToProtectOnPage.push(additionalForm);
                    }
                }

                var renderCaptcha = function(event, form, id) {
                    recaptcha[i] = grecaptcha.render(id, {
                        'theme': 'light',
                        'badge': 'bottomright',
                        'sitekey': '6LeWnKgUAAAAAFCKl2jBAk8iN2y4mhm6UgtuwEX5',
                        'callback': function(token) {
                            if ($(form).valid()) {
                                form.querySelector("[name='amasty_invisible_token']").setAttribute('value', token);
                                $(form).submit();
                            }
                            for (var j = 0; j < recaptcha.length; j++) {
                                grecaptcha.reset(recaptcha[j]);
                            }
                        }
                    });
                };

                for (var i = 0; i < window.formToProtectOnPage.length; i++) {
                    var form = window.formToProtectOnPage[i];
                    if (form.tagName.toLowerCase() != 'form') {
                        continue;
                    }

                    id = form.querySelector("[type='submit']");
                    if (null == id) {
                        if (form.classList.contains('amform-form')) {
                            $(window).on(form.getAttribute('id'), renderCaptcha);
                        } else {
                            console.log(
                                'Amsty Google Invisible reCaptcha: can not protect form with id = '
                                + form.id
                                + ', please remove appropriate URL and Selector in the configuration of the extension.'
                            );
                        }
                        continue;
                    }

                    renderCaptcha(null, form, id);
                }
            };
        });
   </script>

   <script>
    require(['jquery','weltpixel_persistentLayer','weltpixel_gtm', 'Magento_Customer/js/customer-data'],
            function ($, wpPersDl ,wpgtm, customerData) {
                $( document ).ajaxComplete(function( event, xhr, settings ) {
                    if (settings.url.search('/customer\/section\/load/') > 0) {
                        var response = xhr.responseJSON;
                        if (response.gtm) {
                            var dataLayerData = $.parseJSON(response.gtm.datalayer);
                            for (index in dataLayerData) {
                                if(window.dataLayer){
                                    window.dataLayer.push(dataLayerData[index]);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });
                var wpPersDlOptions = {'storageExpiryTime' : 30 };
                var wpGtmOptions = {
                    'enabled' : 1,
                    'persDataLayer' : wpPersDl
                };
                wpPersDl.init(wpPersDlOptions);
                wpgtm.trackPromotion(wpGtmOptions);
                customerData.invalidate(['gtm']);
            });
   </script>
   <script>
    function init_defer(){
                    for(var t=document.getElementsByTagName("iframe"),e=0;e<t.length;e++)
                        t[e].getAttribute("data-src")&&t[e].setAttribute("src",t[e].getAttribute("data-src"));
                }
                window.onload=init_defer;
   </script>
